1/8/25, 11:13 - +91 87972 22242: Creative thinking is the process of approaching problems or situations in an imaginative and innovative way, often leading to solutions or ideas that are both original and effective. It involves stepping outside conventional thought patterns, challenging assumptions, and exploring new perspectives. At its core, creative thinking thrives on curiosity, open-mindedness, and the willingness to embrace uncertainty.

The journey of creative thinking typically starts with curiosity or a desire to solve a problem. This initial spark leads to exploration, where individuals gather information, observe their surroundings, and seek inspiration. During this phase, connections between seemingly unrelated concepts often emerge, laying the foundation for novel ideas. Brainstorming, visualization, and experimentation are tools that help nurture and refine these ideas.

A key component of creative thinking is the ability to view challenges as opportunities rather than obstacles. It demands courage, as new ideas may face skepticism or failure. However, such setbacks are part of the creative process, offering valuable lessons and insights that strengthen and evolve initial concepts.

The culmination of creative thinking is the transformation of abstract ideas into tangible outcomes. These outcomes may manifest as a piece of art, an innovative product, a groundbreaking theory, or a unique solution to a problem. The value of creative thinking lies not only in its end result but also in its capacity to inspire change, spark innovation, and contribute to personal and collective growth.

In conclusion, creative thinking is a dynamic and transformative process that empowers individuals to think beyond limits and create value in unexpected ways. It bridges imagination and reality, encouraging us to see the world not just as it is but as it could be.

1/11/25, 15:01 - +91 87972 22242: Here’s a **quick recap** of your DSA Lab syllabus in concise points to help you memorize easily:

---

### **1. Sorting Techniques**
- **Bubble Sort**: Repeatedly swap adjacent elements if they are in the wrong order. Time: \(O(n^2)\).  
- **Selection Sort**: Find the minimum element and place it in the sorted portion. Time: \(O(n^2)\).  
- **Insertion Sort**: Insert elements into the correct position in a sorted portion. Time: \(O(n^2)\).  
- **Shell Sort**: Variation of insertion sort using a gap sequence. Time: \(O(n^{1.5})\).  
- **Radix Sort**: Non-comparative, sort numbers digit by digit. Time: \(O(d \cdot (n + b))\).  
- **Quick Sort**: Divide and conquer, choose pivot, partition, and sort. Avg: \(O(n \log n)\).

---

### **2. Searching and Hashing Techniques**
- **Linear Search**: Sequential search in the array. Time: \(O(n)\).  
- **Binary Search**: Divide and search in a sorted array. Time: \(O(\log n)\).  
- **Hashing**:
  - **Modulo Division**: Use `key % table_size` to calculate the hash index.  
  - **Digit Extraction**: Combine specific digits (e.g., sum of last two digits).  
  - **Collision Handling**: Use linear probing, chaining, etc.

---

### **3. Stacks**
- **Array Implementation**: Fixed-size stack using an array.  
- **Linked List Implementation**: Dynamically allocate stack nodes.  
- **Applications**:
  - Evaluate **Postfix Expressions** (e.g., `23*4+`).  
  - **Parenthesis Balancing** (e.g., `((a+b))`).  
  - Convert **Infix to Postfix** using precedence rules.

---

### **4. Queues**
- **Ordinary Queue**: FIFO, fixed size, or dynamic (linked list).  
- **Circular Queue**: Rear connects to the front when full.  
- **Priority Queue**: Dequeue based on priority, not order.  
- **Double-Ended Queue**: Insert/delete from both ends.

---

### **5. Linked Lists**
- **Singly Linked List**: Traverse, Insert, Delete, Reverse.  
- **Doubly Linked List**: Traverse in both directions.  
- **Circular Linked List**: Last node connects to the first.  
- Applications: Polynomial addition, comparing arrays vs linked lists.

---

### **6. Trees**
- **Binary Search Tree (BST)**:
  - Create, Insert, Search, Delete nodes.  
  - Traversals:
    - Preorder: Root → Left → Right.  
    - Inorder: Left → Root → Right (Sorted for BST).  
    - Postorder: Left → Right → Root.  
  - Find Largest/Smallest Node, Count Nodes.  

- **Heaps**:
  - **Min Heap**: Parent ≤ Child.  
  - **Max Heap**: Parent ≥ Child.  
  - Operations: Reheap-Up, Reheap-Down.

- **Expression Tree**: Tree representation of expressions (e.g., `a + b * c`).

---

### **7. Graphs**
- Represent using **Adjacency Matrix** or **Adjacency List**.  
- Traversals:
  - **BFS (Breadth-First Search)**: Explore layer by layer.  
  - **DFS (Depth-First Search)**: Explore depth-wise.  
- **Minimum Spanning Tree**:
  - **Prim’s Algorithm**: Greedy, start with any node.  
  - **Kruskal’s Algorithm**: Greedy, process edges in increasing weight.  
- **Shortest Path**: (e.g., Dijkstra’s Algorithm).

---

### Memorization Tips:
- Focus on **time complexities** and **key steps** in each algorithm.  
- Relate applications to real-world scenarios (e.g., stacks for undo, queues for scheduling).  
- For graphs, visualize traversal trees and MST connections.

Let me know if you need help with a specific topic! 😊

2/17/25, 15:34 - +91 93437 73046: *ब्रेकिंग न्यूज़: भूकंप के झटकों से दिल्ली समेत एक महान यूनिवर्सिटी पर असर, AKTU को आया होश!*

दिल्ली-एनसीआर समेत पूरे उत्तर भारत में तेज़ भूकंप के झटकों का असर देखने को मिला। इसी बीच, एक बेहद प्रतिष्ठित यूनिवर्सिटी *AKTU (डॉ. ए.पी.जे. अब्दुल कलाम तकनीकी विश्वविद्यालय)* पर भी इन झटकों का गहरा प्रभाव पड़ा।

सूत्रों के अनुसार, AKTU जो अपनी परीक्षा तारीखों में अप्रत्याशित बदलावों और अंतिम समय पर सूचना देने के लिए कुख्यात है, इस बार भूकंप के झटकों से ऐसा जागा कि परीक्षा स्थगित करने की सूचना एक दिन पहले ही जारी कर दी! छात्रों में इसे लेकर अचंभे और राहत दोनों की भावना देखी गई।

विद्यार्थियों का कहना है कि यह बदलाव किसी चमत्कार से कम नहीं है, क्योंकि आमतौर पर परीक्षा स्थगित होने की सूचना परीक्षा वाले दिन ही मिलती थी। कुछ छात्रों ने इसे "भूकंप से आया प्रशासनिक होश" करार दिया, तो कुछ ने इसे AKTU का ऐतिहासिक मोमेंट बताया।

हालांकि, यूनिवर्सिटी प्रशासन की ओर से यह स्पष्ट नहीं किया गया कि इस जागरूकता का कारण भूकंप था या छात्रों की लगातार शिकायतें। लेकिन एक बात साफ़ है—AKTU में बदलाव की लहर चल रही है, और इसकी जड़ें कहीं न कहीं प्राकृतिक झटकों से जुड़ी हुई हैं।

5/29/25, 10:32 - +91 70110 94476: class A implements Runnable{
    Thread th; 
    boolean suspend_flag, stop_flag;
    sus_res_stop(String tN){
        th=new Thread(this,tN);
        suspend_flag=false;
        stop_flag=false;
        th.start();
    }
    public void run(){
        try{
            int j=1;
            while(++j<20){
                synchronized(this)
                {
                    while(suspend_flag)
                    {
                        wait();
                    }
                    if(stop_flag){
                        break;
                    }
                }
            }
            catch(Exception e){
                System.out.println(e);
            }
        }
        synchronized void suspend(){
            suspend_flag=true;
        }
        synchronized void resume(){
            suspend_flag=false;
            notify();
        }
        synchronized void my_stop(){
            suspend_flag=false;
            stop_flag-true;
            notify();
        }
    }

}
public class runnable_interface1 {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        try {
            A a=new A("SRS");
            System.out.println("Thread A is created & started");
            Thread.sleep(2000);
            a.my_suspend();
            System.out.println("A is suspended");
            Thread.sleep(2000);
            A.my_resume();
            System.out.println("A is resumed");
            Thread.sleep(2000);
            A.my_suspend();
            System.out.println("Thread A is suspended");
            Thread.sleep(2000);
            A.my_resume();
            Thread.sleep(2000);
            A.my_stop();
        
            
        } catch (Exception e) {
        }
    }
    
}

7/1/25, 12:04 - +91 98085 51964: import java.util.LinkedList;
import java.util.Queue;

class ProducerConsumer {
    private final Queue<Integer> queue = new LinkedList<>();
    private final int limit;

    public ProducerConsumer(int limit) {
        this.limit = limit;
    }

    public void produce() throws InterruptedException {
        int value = 0;
        while (true) {
            synchronized (this) {
                while (queue.size() == limit) {
                    wait(); // Wait until there is space in the queue
                }
                queue.add(value);
                System.out.println("Produced: " + value);
                value++;
                notify(); // Notify the consumer that an item has been produced
            }
            Thread.sleep(1000); // Simulate time taken to produce an item
        }
    }

    public void consume() throws InterruptedException {
        while (true) {
            synchronized (this) {
                while (queue.isEmpty()) {
                    wait(); // Wait until there is an item to consume
                }
                int value = queue.poll();
                System.out.println("Consumed: " + value);
                notify(); // Notify the producer that an item has been consumed
            }
            Thread.sleep(1000); // Simulate time taken to consume an item
        }
    }
}

class Producer extends Thread {
    private final ProducerConsumer producerConsumer;

    public Producer(ProducerConsumer producerConsumer) {
        this.producerConsumer = producerConsumer;
    }

    public void run() {
        try {
            producerConsumer.produce();
        } catch (InterruptedException e) {
            Thread.currentThread().interrupt();
        }
    }
}

class Consumer extends Thread {
    private final ProducerConsumer producerConsumer;

    public Consumer(ProducerConsumer producerConsumer) {
        this.producerConsumer = producerConsumer;
    }

    public void run() {
        try {
            producerConsumer.consume();
        } catch (InterruptedException e) {
            Thread.currentThread().interrupt();
        }
    }
}

public class Main {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        ProducerConsumer producerConsumer = new ProducerConsumer(5); // Limit of 5 items in the queue

        Producer producer = new Producer(producerConsumer);
        Consumer consumer = new Consumer(producerConsumer);

        producer.start();
        consumer.start();
    }
}

interface Drawable {
    void draw();
}

// Circle class implementing Drawable interface
class Circle implements Drawable {
    @Override
    public void draw() {
        System.out.println("Drawing a Circle");
    }
}

// Rectangle class implementing Drawable interface
class Rectangle implements Drawable {
    @Override
    public void draw() {
        System.out.println("Drawing a Rectangle");
    }
}

// Triangle class implementing Drawable interface
class Triangle implements Drawable {
    @Override
    public void draw() {
        System.out.println("Drawing a Triangle");
    }
}

// Main class to test the implementation
public class Main {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        Drawable circle = new Circle();
        Drawable rectangle = new Rectangle();
        Drawable triangle = new Triangle();

        circle.draw();      // Output: Drawing a Circle
        rectangle.draw();   // Output: Drawing a Rectangle
        triangle.draw();    // Output: Drawing a Triangle
    }
}
